This allows any INI setting to be overridden via environment variables following the GF_* naming convention.\\n\\n**Configuration Value Expansion**: The expandConfig() function in pkg/setting/expanders.go processes configuration values that contain variable references. This allows any INI setting to be overridden via environment variables following the GF_* naming convention.\\n\\n**Configuration Value Expansion**: The expandConfig() function in pkg/setting/expanders.go processes configuration values that contain variable references. It supports environment variable expansion via envExpander and file content expansion via fileExpander, using a regex pattern to identify expandable values marked with $(VARIABLE) or $__file(FILEPATH) syntax.\\n\\n**Sensitive Value Masking**: The RedactedValue() function in pkg/setting/setting.go (line 660) implements the masking/redaction logic.
